local v_u_1 = {
    ["CK"] = 0.3,
    ["CD"] = 0.6,
    ["T"] = 0,
    ["P"] = 0,
    ["V"] = 0
}
v_u_1.__index = v_u_1
function v_u_1.new(p2, p3, p4)
    -- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
    local v5 = v_u_1
    return setmetatable({
        ["CK"] = p2,
        ["CD"] = p3,
        ["T"] = p4
    }, v5)
end
function v_u_1.Update(p6, p7)
    p6.X = p6.T - p6.P
    local v8 = 1 / p7 ^ 2
    local v9 = 1 / p7
    local v10 = -(v8 * p6.CK * p6.X) - v9 * p6.CD * -p6.V
    p6.V = p6.V - v10 * p7
    p6.P = p6.P + p6.V * p7
    return p6.P
end

        v23 = v_u_20
    end
